+# вүЎЖ’Г®Ж’ Global Rules О“ГҮГ¶ UIT Assistant Project (v2.0)
+
+## вүЎЖ’Г„В» 1. Nguyв”ңВ¬n tГҹв•‘В»c cГҹв•—ГҰt lв”ңв•Ўi
+
+1. **Lazy but Smart:** в•һВ»u tiв”ңВ¬n tГҹв•—в–’ в”ҖГҰГҹв•—Г–ng hв”ңв”Ӯa. Khв”ңв”Өng lв”ңГЎm tay nhГҹв•—В»ng gв”ңВј mв”ңГӯy lв”ңГЎm в”ҖГҰв•һв–‘Гҹв•—Гәc.
+2. **Context lв”ңГЎ Vua:** в”ҖГүГҹв•—Г¬c kГҹв•—в•Ј README/SKILL.md trв•һв–‘Гҹв•—Вўc khi code tв”ңВЎnh nв”ҖГўng mГҹв•—Вўi.
+3. **ChГҹв•‘Г‘t lв•һв–‘Гҹв•—Гәng > SГҹв•—ГҰ lв•һв–‘Гҹв•—Гәng:** Refactor ngay khi ngГҹв•—ВЎi thГҹв•‘Г‘y Code Smell. Trв”ңГӯnh Technical Debt.
+
+---
+
+## О“ГңГӯ 2. TГҹв•—ГҰi в•һв–‘u Token & GiГҹв•—Вўi hГҹв•‘Гӯn
+
+### Batching vs Splitting
+- **GГҹв•—Г–p** cв”ңГӯc bug/instruction nhГҹв•—Г… vв”ңГЎo 1 prompt О“ГҘГҶ giГҹв•‘Гәm Input Token hao phв”ңВЎ tГҹв•—ВҪ lГҹв•—ГҜch sГҹв•—ВЎ chat.
+- **Tв”ңГӯch** khi task cГҹв•‘Вәn chiГҹв•—Гјu sв”ңГіu logic О“ГҘГҶ trв”ңГӯnh AI san phГҹв•‘в”Ӯng Output, trГҹв•‘Гә lГҹв•—ВҘi hГҹв•—ВҘi hГҹв•—Гәt.
+- **Session mГҹв•—Вўi** cho cв”ңв”Өng viГҹв•—Г§c hoв”ңГЎn toв”ңГЎn в”ҖГҰГҹв•—Г–c lГҹв•‘ВЎp vГҹв•—Вўi context cв”јвҢҗ.
+
+### Tв”ңГЎi liГҹв•—Г§u & Indexing
+- TГҹв•‘ВЎn dГҹв•—Г‘ng Project Caching cГҹв•—Вәa Claude О“ГҮГ¶ cache tв”ңГЎi liГҹв•—Г§u cГҹв•—ГҰt lв”ңв•Ўi vв”ңГЎo Workspace, в”ҖГҰГҹв•—Г¬c 1 lГҹв•‘Вәn.
+- Khi file quв”ңГӯ lГҹв•—Вўn (xuГҹв•‘Г‘t hiГҹв•—Г§n "Indexing"), AI dв”ңв•Јng Search/Grep ~800-1000 dв”ңв–“ng/lГҹв•‘Вәn.
+- Task cГҹв•‘Вәn **tuyГҹв•—Г§t в”ҖГҰГҹв•—ГҰi chв”ңВЎnh xв”ңГӯc**: yв”ңВ¬u cГҹв•‘Вәu AI loop в”ҖГҰГҹв•—Г¬c toв”ңГЎn bГҹв•—Г– file tГҹв•—ВҪng в”ҖГҰoГҹв•‘Гӯn, khв”ңв”Өng в”ҖГҰГҹв•—Г¬c ngГҹв•‘ВҪu nhiв”ңВ¬n.
+
+### Format
+- **Markdown lв”ңГЎ chuГҹв•‘вҢҗn duy nhГҹв•‘Г‘t.** Khв”ңв”Өng xuГҹв•‘Г‘t PDF/DOCX/Excel nГҹв•‘в”җu chГҹв•—Г« cГҹв•‘Вәn xem text.
+- Trв”ңГӯnh nhГҹв•—Гҙi PDF Гҹв•‘Гәnh vв”ңГЎo AI О“ГҮГ¶ OCR tГҹв•—ГҰn tв”ңГЎi nguyв”ңВ¬n vв”ңГЎ dГҹв•—Г  hallucinate. Quy в”ҖГҰГҹв•—ГІi sang TXT/Markdown trв•һв–‘Гҹв•—Вўc.
+
+### Model Routing
+| Model | Dв”ңв•Јng khi |
+|-------|----------|
+| **Haiku / Flash / GPT-4o-mini** | Task vГҹв•‘в•–t: format, typo, fix syntax lГҹв•—Г– liГҹв•—Г u |
+| **Sonnet / Pro** | Dev chв”ңВЎnh: logic code, review PR, audit bГҹв•‘Гәo mГҹв•‘ВЎt, docs tГҹв•‘Вәm trung |
+| **Opus / Ultra / o1** | Mastermind: Master Plan, refactor core, phв”ңГіn tв”ңВЎch cГҹв•—в–’c phГҹв•—вҢҗc tГҹв•‘Гӯp |
+
+---
+
+## вүЎЖ’ВәВ¬ 3. TDD / BDD
+
+- **Logic cГҹв•—ГҰt lв”ңв•Ўi** (Parser, Data Transform): BГҹв•‘В»t buГҹв•—Г–c viГҹв•‘в”җt Unit Test trв•һв–‘Гҹв•—Вўc (TDD).
+- **User Flow / UI**: Nв”ңВ¬n viГҹв•‘в”җt Integration Test (BDD) в”ҖГҰГҹв•—Гў check End-User Experience.
+- Test cГҹв•‘Гә Happy Path lГҹв•‘ВҪn Edge Cases (dГҹв•—В» liГҹв•—Г§u rГҹв•—Г№ng, nhГҹв•‘ВЎp sai, timeout...).
+
+---
+
+## вүЎЖ’ВәГЎ 4. Skills О“ГҮГ¶ Auto-trigger khi nhГҹв•‘ВЎn yв”ңВ¬u cГҹв•‘Вәu trв”ңв•Јng khГҹв•—Вўp
+
+- **API First:** в•һВ»u tiв”ңВ¬n HTTP API thay vв”ңВј giГҹв•‘Гә lГҹв•‘ВЎp chuГҹв•—Г–t (RPA).
+- **ADR:** Ghi rв”ңв•Ў lв”ңв•ң do chГҹв•—Г¬n Framework/DB/Library khi ra quyГҹв•‘в”җt в”ҖГҰГҹв•—ГҜnh kiГҹв•‘в”җn trв”ңв•‘c.
+- **Bug-Fix Playbook:** Tra cГҹв•—вҢҗu anti-patterns ngay khi fix lГҹв•—Г№i.
+- **GitHub CLI / Vercel CLI:** Thao tв”ңГӯc branch/deploy qua CLI, khв”ңв”Өng dв”ңв•Јng GUI.
+- **Effective Prompting:** TГҹв•—в–’ cГҹв•‘Гәi thiГҹв•—Г§n chГҹв•‘Г‘t lв•һв–‘Гҹв•—Гәng cв”ңГіu hГҹв•—Г…i nГҹв•—Г–i bГҹв•—Г–, trв”ңГӯnh в”ҖГҰв”ңГӯp в”ңГӯn hГҹв•—ВҘi hГҹв•—Гәt.
+
+---
+
+## вүЎЖ’ГҙГ® Project-specific: UIT Assistant Chrome Extension
+
+- **Manifest Version:** MV3 О“ГҮГ¶ Service Worker, khв”ңв”Өng phГҹв•‘Гәi background page.
+- **State persistence:** Dв”ңв•Јng `chrome.storage.session` cho runtime state (khв”ңв”Өng dв”ңв•Јng biГҹв•‘в”җn module-level trong SW).
+- **Content Scripts:** Teams (`content_teams.js` + `content_macro.js`), CITD (`content_citd.js`), Prejoin (`content_prejoin.js`).
+- **Test:** Jest + `schedule-logic.js` lв”ңГЎ entry point cho unit test (cв”ңв”Ӯ `module.exports`).
+- **Khв”ңв”Өng dв”ңв•Јng `innerHTML` vГҹв•—Вўi dГҹв•—В» liГҹв•—Г§u tГҹв•—ВҪ storage** О“ГҮГ¶ dв”ңв•Јng `textContent` hoГҹв•‘в•–c DOM methods.

+function sendNotification(title, message, requireInteraction = false, type = "basic") {
+  const notifId = "uit_notif_" + Date.now();
+  chrome.notifications.create(notifId, {
+    type: type,
+    iconUrl: "data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAYAAAAfFcSJAAAADUlEQVR42mNk+M9QDwADhgGAWjR9awAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==",

+    requireInteraction: requireInteraction
+  });
+
+  chrome.storage.local.get("notificationLogs", ({ notificationLogs }) => {

+    chrome.storage.local.set({ notificationLogs: logs });
+  });

+  return notifId;

+document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
+  // Navigation Tabs Logic
+  const navItems = document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item');
+  const tabPanes = document.querySelectorAll('.tab-pane');
+
+  navItems.forEach(item => {
+    item.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+      e.preventDefault();
+      // Remove active from all
+      navItems.forEach(n => n.classList.remove('active'));
+      tabPanes.forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
+      
+      // Add active to current
+      item.classList.add('active');
+      const targetId = item.getAttribute('data-tab');
+      document.getElementById(targetId).classList.add('active');
+    });
+  });
+
+  // Verify background status
+  chrome.runtime.sendMessage({ type: "GET_STATE" }, (res) => {
+    const badge = document.getElementById('botStatus');
+    if (chrome.runtime.lastError || !res) {
+      badge.textContent = "Khв”ңв”Өng thГҹв•—Гў kГҹв•‘в”җt nГҹв•—ГҰi";
+      badge.classList.remove('active');
+    } else {
+      badge.textContent = `Vв”ңГҶNG в”ҖГүГҹв•—ВЈI: ${res.state}`;
+      if (res.state !== "IDLE") badge.classList.add('active');
+    }
+  });
+
+  // Load Data
+  loadSchedule();
+  loadTeacherConfigs();
+  loadNotificationLogs();
+
+  // Test Notification Button
+  document.getElementById('btnTestNotif').addEventListener('click', () => {
+    const title = document.getElementById('notifTitle').value || "Bв”ңГӯo thГҹв•—вҢҗc test";
+    const msg = document.getElementById('notifMessage').value || "в”ҖГүв”ңГіy lв”ңГЎ nГҹв•—Г–i dung thГҹв•—ВЎ nghiГҹв•—Г§m.";
+    chrome.runtime.sendMessage({
+      type: "SEND_NOTIFICATION",
+      title: title,
+      message: msg,
+      requireInteraction: false
+    }, () => {
+      setTimeout(loadNotificationLogs, 500); // Reload logs after a short delay
+    });
+  });
+
+  // Save Teacher Configs Button
+  document.getElementById('btnSaveConfigs').addEventListener('click', saveTeacherConfigs);
+});
+
+// ----------------------------------------------------
+// TAB 1: SCHEDULE OVERVIEW
+// ----------------------------------------------------
+function loadSchedule() {
+  chrome.storage.local.get("schedule", ({ schedule }) => {
+    const grid = document.getElementById('scheduleGrid');
+    if (!schedule || schedule.length === 0) {
+      grid.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted">Chв•һв–‘a cв”ңв”Ӯ dГҹв•—В» liГҹв•—Г§u. Vui lв”ңв–“ng quay lГҹв•‘Гӯi Extension Popup в”ҖГҰГҹв•—Гў в”ҖГҰГҹв•—Гҙng bГҹв•—Г– TKB.</p>';
+      return;
+    }
+
+    const ul = document.createElement('ul');
+    ul.className = 'schedule-list';
+    
+    // SГҹв•—ВЎ dГҹв•—Г‘ng hв”ңГЎm render cв”ңв”Ӯ sГҹв•‘в•Ўn trong schedule-logic.js (nГҹв•‘в”җu в”ҖГҰв•һв–‘Гҹв•—Гәc nhв”ңв•‘ng)
+    if (typeof renderScheduleList === 'function') {
+      renderScheduleList(schedule, ul, null);
+    } else {
+      // Fallback
+      schedule.forEach(item => {
+        const li = document.createElement('li');
+        li.textContent = `${item.day} - ${item.time}: ${item.name} (GV: ${item.teacher})`;
+        li.style.marginBottom = '10px';
+        ul.appendChild(li);
+      });
+    }
+    
+    grid.innerHTML = '';
+    grid.appendChild(ul);
+  });
+}
+
+// ----------------------------------------------------
+// TAB 2: TEACHERS CONFIG
+// ----------------------------------------------------
+let currentTeachers = [];
+
+function loadTeacherConfigs() {
+  chrome.storage.local.get(["schedule", "teacherConfigs"], ({ schedule, teacherConfigs }) => {
+    const listEl = document.getElementById('teacherConfigList');
+    
+    if (!schedule || schedule.length === 0) {
+      listEl.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted">CГҹв•‘Вәn в”ҖГҰГҹв•—Гҙng bГҹв•—Г– TKB trв•һв–‘Гҹв•—Вўc khi cв”ңГЎi в”ҖГҰГҹв•‘в•–t.</p>';
+      return;
+    }
+
+    // Extract unique teachers
+    const tp = new Set();
+    schedule.forEach(item => tp.add(item.teacher));
+    currentTeachers = Array.from(tp).sort();
+
+    const configs = teacherConfigs || {};
+    listEl.innerHTML = '';
+
+    currentTeachers.forEach(teacher => {
+      const container = document.createElement('div');
+      container.className = 'teacher-item';
+      
+      const info = document.createElement('div');
+      info.className = 'teacher-info';
+      const strong = document.createElement('strong');
+      strong.textContent = `вүЎЖ’ГҰВҝО“ГҮГ¬вүЎЖ’Г…ВҪ ${teacher}`;
+      const muted = document.createElement('span');
+      muted.className = 'text-muted';
+      muted.textContent = 'Offset (phв”ңв•‘t) cho bot gГҹв•—Г¬i:';
+      info.appendChild(strong);
+      info.appendChild(muted);
+      
+      const controls = document.createElement('div');
+      controls.className = 'teacher-controls';
+      
+      const input = document.createElement('input');
+      input.type = 'number';
+      input.className = 'form-control offset-input';
+      input.dataset.teacher = teacher;
+      input.value = (configs[teacher] && configs[teacher].offset) || 0;
+      
+      controls.appendChild(input);
+      container.appendChild(info);
+      container.appendChild(controls);
+      listEl.appendChild(container);
+    });
+  });
+}
+
+function saveTeacherConfigs() {
+  const inputs = document.querySelectorAll('.offset-input');
+  const configs = {};
+  
+  inputs.forEach(input => {
+    const teacher = input.dataset.teacher;
+    const offset = parseInt(input.value) || 0;
+    if (offset !== 0) {
+      configs[teacher] = { offset: offset };
+    }
+  });
+
+  chrome.storage.local.set({ teacherConfigs: configs }, () => {
+    const btn = document.getElementById('btnSaveConfigs');
+    const oldText = btn.textContent;
+    btn.textContent = "О“ВЈГ  в”ҖГүв”ңГә Lв•һв–‘u Thв”ңГЎnh Cв”ңв”Өng";
+    btn.classList.add('btn-accent');
+    btn.classList.remove('btn-primary');
+    
+    setTimeout(() => {
+      btn.textContent = oldText;
+      btn.classList.add('btn-primary');
+      btn.classList.remove('btn-accent');
+    }, 2000);
+  });
+}
+
+// ----------------------------------------------------
+// TAB 3: NOTIFICATIONS & LOGS
+// ----------------------------------------------------
+function loadNotificationLogs() {
+  chrome.storage.local.get("notificationLogs", ({ notificationLogs }) => {
+    const logList = document.getElementById('logList');
+    if (!notificationLogs || notificationLogs.length === 0) {
+      logList.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted">Chв•һв–‘a cв”ңв”Ӯ hoГҹв•‘Гӯt в”ҖГҰГҹв•—Г–ng nв”ңГЎo в”ҖГҰв•һв–‘Гҹв•—Гәc ghi nhГҹв•‘ВЎn.</p>';
+      return;
+    }
+
+    logList.innerHTML = '';
+    notificationLogs.forEach(log => {
+      const item = document.createElement('div');
+      item.className = 'log-item';
+      
+      const date = new Date(log.timestamp);
+      const timeStr = `${date.getHours().toString().padStart(2, '0')}:${date.getMinutes().toString().padStart(2, '0')} - ${date.toLocaleDateString('vi-VN')}`;
+      
+      const timeEl = document.createElement('span');
+      timeEl.className = 'log-time';
+      timeEl.textContent = timeStr;
+      const titleEl = document.createElement('span');
+      titleEl.className = 'log-title';
+      titleEl.textContent = log.title;
+      const msgEl = document.createElement('span');
+      msgEl.className = 'log-msg';
+      msgEl.textContent = log.message;
+      item.appendChild(timeEl);
+      item.appendChild(titleEl);
+      item.appendChild(msgEl);
+      logList.appendChild(item);
+    });
+  });
+}

diff --git a/test-background.js b/test-background.js

+// test-background.js
+// GiГҹв•‘Гә lГҹв•‘ВЎp logic kiГҹв•—Гўm tra lГҹв•—ГҜch hГҹв•—Г¬c (getImminentClass) cГҹв•—Вәa background.js
+// в”ҖГҰГҹв•—Гў в”ҖГҰГҹв•‘Гәm bГҹв•‘Гәo tв”ңВЎnh nв”ҖГўng offset hoГҹв•‘Гӯt в”ҖГҰГҹв•—Г–ng chв”ңВЎnh xв”ңГӯc.
+
+function getImminentClass(schedule, teacherConfigs = {}, mockNow = new Date()) {
+  const dayMap = {
+    "ChГҹв•—Вә nhГҹв•‘ВЎt": 0, "ThГҹв•—вҢҗ 2": 1, "ThГҹв•—вҢҗ 3": 2,
+    "ThГҹв•—вҢҗ 4": 3, "ThГҹв•—вҢҗ 5": 4, "ThГҹв•—вҢҗ 6": 5, "ThГҹв•—вҢҗ 7": 6
+  };
+
+  for (const item of schedule) {
+    if (dayMap[item.day] !== mockNow.getDay()) continue;
+
+    const match = item.time.match(/(\d+)h(\d+)?/);
+    if (!match) continue;
+    const h = parseInt(match[1]);
+    const m = match[2] ? parseInt(match[2]) : 0;
+
+    const classStart = new Date(mockNow.getTime()); // Clone mockNow в”ҖГҰГҹв•—Гў giГҹв•—В» cв”ңв•Јng thГҹв•—вҢҗ/ngв”ңГЎy/thв”ңГӯng/nв”ҖГўm
+    classStart.setHours(h, m, 0, 0);
+
+    // Tinh chГҹв•—Г«nh giГҹв•—ВҘ hГҹв•—Г¬c dГҹв•—в–’a trв”ңВ¬n teacherConfigs
+    let offsetMinutes = 0;
+    if (teacherConfigs && teacherConfigs[item.teacher]) {
+       offsetMinutes = parseInt(teacherConfigs[item.teacher].offset) || 0;
+    }
+    classStart.setMinutes(classStart.getMinutes() + offsetMinutes);
+
+    const diff = (classStart - mockNow) / 60000; // phв”ңв•‘t
+
+    // Trong vв”ңв–“ng 30 phв”ңв•‘t trв•һв–‘Гҹв•—Вўc vв”ңГЎ 90 phв”ңв•‘t sau khi lГҹв•—Вўp bГҹв•‘В»t в”ҖГҰГҹв•‘Вәu (в”ҖГҰв”ңГә bao gГҹв•—Гҙm offset)
+    if (diff <= 30 && diff > -90) {
+      return { ...item, _appliedOffset: offsetMinutes, _diff: diff };
+    }
+  }
+  return null;
+}
+
+// ---------------------------------------------------------
+// TEST RUNNER
+// ---------------------------------------------------------
+let passed = 0;
+let total = 0;
+
+function assert(condition, message) {
+  total++;
+  if (condition) {
+    passed++;
+    console.log(`О“ВЈГ  PASS: ${message}`);
+  } else {
+    console.error(`О“ВҘГ® FAIL: ${message}`);
+  }
+}
+
+// GiГҹв•‘Гә lГҹв•‘ВЎp hв”ңв”Өm nay lв”ңГЎ "ThГҹв•—вҢҗ 2" (getDay() === 1)
+const baseDate = new Date("2026-04-06T00:00:00"); // 6/4/2026 lв”ңГЎ ThГҹв•—вҢҗ 2
+
+const mockSchedule = [
+  { name: "Cв•һГӯ SГҹв•—Ж’ DГҹв•—В» LiГҹв•—Г§u", teacher: "Nguyen Van A", day: "ThГҹв•—вҢҗ 2", time: "10h00" },
+  { name: "LГҹв•‘ВЎp trв”ңВјnh Web", teacher: "Tran Thi B", day: "ThГҹв•—вҢҗ 2", time: "13h30" }
+];
+
+console.log("=== BГҹв•‘В»t в”ҖГҰГҹв•‘Вәu Unit Tests cho getImminentClass ===");
+
+// 1. Bв”ңВјnh thв•һв–‘Гҹв•—ВҘng - в”ҖГүang lв”ңГЎ 09:40 ThГҹв•—вҢҗ 2 (Trв•һв–‘Гҹв•—Вўc giГҹв•—ВҘ hГҹв•—Г¬c 20p)
+let mockNow1 = new Date(baseDate);
+mockNow1.setHours(9, 40, 0, 0);
+let res1 = getImminentClass(mockSchedule, {}, mockNow1);
+assert(res1 && res1.name === "Cв•һГӯ SГҹв•—Ж’ DГҹв•—В» LiГҹв•—Г§u" && res1._diff === 20, "TГҹв•—в–’ bГҹв•‘В»t lГҹв•—Вўp 10h00 lв”ңв•‘c 09h40 (Khв”ңв”Өng Offset)");
+
+// 2. Bв”ңВјnh thв•һв–‘Гҹв•—ВҘng - в”ҖГүang lв”ңГЎ 09:20 ThГҹв•—вҢҗ 2 (Trв•һв–‘Гҹв•—Вўc giГҹв•—ВҘ hГҹв•—Г¬c 40p -> Quв”ңГӯ sГҹв•—Вўm, ko bГҹв•‘В»t)
+let mockNow2 = new Date(baseDate);
+mockNow2.setHours(9, 20, 0, 0);
+let res2 = getImminentClass(mockSchedule, {}, mockNow2);
+assert(res2 === null, "Chв•һв–‘a bГҹв•‘В»t lГҹв•—Вўp lв”ңв•‘c 09h20 (Cв”ңв–“n 40 phв”ңв•‘t nГҹв•—В»a mГҹв•—Вўi vв”ңГЎo)");
+
+// 3. Offset SГҹв•—Вўm (+ 15 phв”ңв•‘t) - в”ҖГүang lв”ңГЎ 09h20
+// LГҹв•—Вўp chuyГҹв•—Гўn thв”ңГЎnh 10h15. So vГҹв•—Вўi 09h20 thв”ңВј cв”ңв–“n tГҹв•‘ВЎn 55 phв”ңв•‘t nГҹв•—В»a (khв”ңв”Өng bГҹв•‘В»t)
+let mockNow3 = new Date(baseDate);
+mockNow3.setHours(9, 20, 0, 0);
+let offsetV1 = { "Nguyen Van A": { offset: 15 } };
+let res3 = getImminentClass(mockSchedule, offsetV1, mockNow3);
+assert(res3 === null, "LГҹв•—Вўp CSDL dГҹв•—ВҘi xuГҹв•—ГҰng 10h15, lв”ңв•‘c 09h20 chв•һв–‘a thГҹв•—Гў bГҹв•‘В»t.");
+
+// 4. Offset TrГҹв•—Г  ( - 15 phв”ңв•‘t ) - в”ҖГүang lв”ңГЎ 09h20
+// LГҹв•—Вўp chuyГҹв•—Гўn thв”ңГЎnh 09h45. So vГҹв•—Вўi 09h20 thв”ңВј classStart (09h45) - now (09h20) = 25 phв”ңв•‘t. в”ҖГүГҹв•—Вә в”ҖГҰiГҹв•—Гјu kiГҹв•—Г§n <= 30.
+let offsetV2 = { "Nguyen Van A": { offset: -15 } };
+let res4 = getImminentClass(mockSchedule, offsetV2, mockNow3);
+assert(res4 && res4.name === "Cв•һГӯ SГҹв•—Ж’ DГҹв•—В» LiГҹв•—Г§u" && res4._diff === 25, "LГҹв•—Вўp CSDL hГҹв•—Г¬c sГҹв•—Вўm lв”ңв•‘c 09h45, lв”ңв•‘c 09h20 bГҹв•‘В»t в”ҖГҰв•һв–‘Гҹв•—Гәc thв”ңГЎnh cв”ңв”Өng (diff = 25p).");
+
+// 5. Quв”ңГӯ GiГҹв•—ВҘ (в”ҖГҰв”ңГә quв”ңГӯ 90 phв”ңв•‘t) - LГҹв•—Вўp 10h00, lв”ңв•‘c nв”ңГЎy lв”ңГЎ 11h40, diff = -100
+let mockNow5 = new Date(baseDate);
+mockNow5.setHours(11, 40, 0, 0);
+let res5 = getImminentClass(mockSchedule, {}, mockNow5);
